Amidst News of New Cotton Hitting the Market, Japanese Factories Send Personnel to the Countryside to Purchase; 44 Japanese Factories in China Have a Total of 1.9 Million Spindles

A Hua Dong News Agency report states that the first estimate for this year's new cotton crop is over 16 million dan (a unit of weight), a one-third increase compared to last year's bumper harvest. As news of the new cotton crop hitting the market spreads, Japanese yarn factories in China are following the old tricks of the Japanese grain industry, sending personnel to the countryside to purchase cotton. It is reported that there are now 44 Japanese yarn factories throughout China. Due to the advantageous situation of operating continuously throughout the year, their production volume from the current 1,944,504 spindles is already comparable to that of domestic factories. Therefore, they are even more actively purchasing raw cotton.

Purchasing This Year's New Cotton in the Countryside

This year's new cotton, excluding the Yuyao cotton which has already hit the market, will have samples of the Lingbin cotton available around the seventh lunar month. In addition to the provinces of Hebei, Chahar, Shanxi, and Shandong, which have already been forcibly annexed by Japanese yarn factories in China, the 30 Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai have also sent personnel to cotton-producing areas in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces to encourage local cotton merchants to purchase cotton. The prices they offer are higher than the general selling prices. It is rumored that they plan to purchase one million dan of cotton this year.

44 Japanese Factories Throughout China

Currently, there are 44 Japanese yarn factories within China. A. Within Shanghai: 1. Shanghai Textile Co., Ltd. (5 factories), 2. Nichi-Ka (China-Japan) Textile Co., Ltd. (8 factories), 3. Naigaiwata (Inland and Overseas Cotton) Co., Ltd. (9 factories), 4. Tong Hwa (East China) Textile Co., Ltd. (1 factory), 5. Toa (East Asia) Textile Co., Ltd. (2 factories), Gongda (Public and Great) (2 factories), Datong Yarn Factory, Toyota Textile Factory, and Yufeng Textile Co., Ltd., totaling 30 factories. In Qingdao: Naigaiwata Yarn Factory, Fuji Yarn Factory, Gongda No. 5 Factory, Longxing Yarn Factory, Baolai Yarn Factory, Dakang Yarn Factory, Shanghai Textile Qingdao Factory, Toa Textile Qingdao Factory, and Toyota Qingdao Factory, totaling 10 factories. Also, Wuhan Taian Textile Co., Ltd., Naigaiwata Co., Ltd., and Dalian Futian Yarn Factory, making a total of 44 factories.

Rapid Increase in Spindles to Compete with Us

The 44 Japanese yarn factories in China now have 1,944,504 spindles. They plan to add another 20,720 spindles, 340,356 thread spindles, 23,127 looms, and plan to add 1,152 looms. They have 88,828 kilowatts of electric power, 14,025 horsepower of steam power, 68,683 workers, use 3,405,408 dan of cotton, produce 546,797 bales of yarn, and 633,861,000 square yards of cloth. Due to the fact that one-fourth of our country's 2,850,745 spindles are idle, Japanese yarn is already able to compete with us.

Banking and Money Industries Initiate the Organization of an Amateur Association; A General Membership Meeting Was Held Yesterday

The Banking and Money Industries Amateur Association, organized by members of the banking and money industries in Shanghai, began preparations in July. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the first general membership meeting was held on the third floor of the YMCA on Sichuan Road. About 60-70 people from the banking and money industries attended. Banks such as the Bank of China, Shanghai Bank, Shanghai Municipal Bank, Yien Yieh (Salt Industry) Bank, Kincheng Bank, Continental Bank, Zhongnan Bank, and Zhejiang Industrial Bank, among over 20 others, all had representatives in attendance. Xie Shuren, the initiator of the association, was nominated as the temporary chairman to report on the progress of the association's preparations and to discuss issues related to recruiting members. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. The association's declaration, charter, and list of names are published below.

Declaration: The Banking and Money Industries Amateur Association's First General Membership Declaration: Since we initiated the organization of the Shanghai Banking and Money Industries Amateur Association and issued our opinion letter, we have immediately received enthusiastic support from colleagues in the banking and money industries, and they have offered numerous suggestions, encouraging the early establishment of this association. This enthusiasm has given us great assistance, and we must thank all of our fellow members. After more than a month of planning by the initiators and enthusiastic encouragement from the members, the preparatory meeting was finally held on the afternoon of July 26 at the YMCA auditorium. At that time, the draft charter was passed (see below), and 11 preparatory committee members were elected to begin preparing everything. All of the association's affairs are progressing actively. However, we realize that the strength of a few people is limited, and the advancement of all work, whether in terms of material or human resources, requires the support of everyone. Secondly, we also recognize that in the past, our contact with fellow members has been insufficient, and many people may not even know about this association, which has led to less enthusiastic participation, especially in the money industry. For this reason, the preparatory committee decided to establish a special recruiting committee and decided to immediately begin a recruiting campaign so that every colleague working in the banking and money industries would have the opportunity to participate. We believe that this recruiting campaign is of great significance. It is the assistant and supporter that will enable this association to be established quickly. Enthusiastic members, please do your best to promote this recruiting campaign! We welcome all colleagues in the banking and money industries to participate.

Association Charter: Draft Charter of the Banking and Money Industries Amateur Association: 1. Name: Shanghai Banking and Money Industries Amateur Association. 2. Purpose: To connect emotions, exchange knowledge, improve amateur life, and enhance service efficiency. 3. Address: The association's address will be located in the central district. 4. Membership: All colleagues serving in the Shanghai banking and money industries, regardless of gender or age, are eligible to become members. 5. Membership Fees: A. Membership Fee: A one-time entrance fee of one yuan will be collected upon joining and will not be collected again. Regular expenses will be determined at the general meeting, but shall not exceed half a yuan per month. Donations: With the approval of the board of directors, special fundraising activities may be held. B. Funds: Raised externally in the name of the association. 6. General Meeting: The General Membership Meeting is the highest authority of the association, holding a regular meeting once a year. When necessary, a special meeting may be convened by the board of directors upon the proposal of one-third of the members. 7. Directors: Eleven directors will be elected by the General Membership Meeting to handle the various affairs of the association. Well-known figures in the banking and money industries will be appointed by the board of directors as honorary directors. 8. Supervisors: Three supervisors will be elected by the General Membership Meeting to supervise the association's affairs. 9. Term of Office: The term of office for directors and supervisors is one year, and they may be re-elected. 10. The Board of Directors shall elect a chairman and appoint persons in charge of each department. The Board of Directors shall meet once a month, and supervisors may attend. The organization of each department is as follows: A. General Affairs Department: Accounting, documents, general affairs, statistics, etc. B. Public Relations Department: Public relations, investigations, etc. C. Academic Department: Remedial education, library, reading room, lectures, academic research, etc. D. Entertainment Department: Music, Peking opera, drama, travel, dinners, photography, etc. E. Sports Department: Soccer, tennis, basketball, ping pong, swimming, etc. F. Publications Department: Editing, publishing, and distribution, etc. 11. Secretaries: The Board of Directors may hire a number of secretaries from among the members to assist in the affairs of each department. 12. Supplementary Provisions: 1. The organization and detailed rules of each department will be determined separately. 2. If there are any imperfections in this charter, they may be proposed by one-third of the members and amended with the approval of the General Meeting.

Hiring Team Leaders: The association sent a letter to various team leaders, stating: "Dear Sir, In order to expand membership recruitment, we plan to hire several team leaders to facilitate the process. We know that you strongly agree with the purpose of this association, and we are hereby sending you a special letter inviting you to serve as a recruitment team leader. We hope you will introduce us widely. With anticipation." The hired team leaders include: Tang Kechang of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Qu Huoxin of Shanghai Women's Bank, Ni Zhiqing of Nanjing Road Jiaotong Bank, Fang Mayin of Qiye (Enterprise) Bank, Yu Xiangzhen of Nonggong (Farmers and Workers) Bank, Zhou Xinbai of Siming Bank, Cao Tingsong of Guohua Bank, Zhong Zimin of the Silk Industry Bank, Yuan Rongfang of Jiangsu Bank, Zhao Zuqing, Zhu Qikang of Zhongfu Bank, Yan Shoutang of Yien Yieh Bank, Ni Xiaoben of Bank of China, Guo Junquan of Commercial Bank, Yu Fumin of Tonghe Bank, Wang Peiji of Zhongyi Trust, Bao Jiarui of Shanghai Bank, Zhang Rukun, Cai Zhifan, Gan Hongtao of Central Trust Bureau, Fang Yicheng of Tianyi Insurance, Zhuang Bin of Anping Insurance, Li Jinbo of Yumin Bank, Hu Zhijun of Siming Insurance, Yan Shouyong of Yongda Bank, Guo Chuanfa of Datong Bank, Jin Zhehe of Huayi Bank, Shao Guizhen of Banque de l'Indochine, Liu Shizhong of Zhongnan Bank, Fan Jinhui of Zhonghui Bank, Zhang Huaixuan of Hengli Bank, Jiang Meixi of Guoxin Bank, and Ling Yunqi of Bank of China National Products.

Jieshun Fish Company Files Appeal; Ministry of Industry Dismisses It

The Jieshun Fish Company of this city filed an appeal with the Ministry of Industry regarding the illegality of the Shanghai Fish Market regulations. The Ministry of Industry's appeal decision No. 226 is as follows: Main Text: The appeal is dismissed. Facts: The appellant, in May of this year, saw in various Shanghai daily newspapers the Ministry's announcement No. 416, stating that the Shanghai Fish Market established by the Ministry was operated according to the public-private joint operation method approved by the Central Political Conference and that the regulations of the Shanghai Fish Market Co., Ltd., a public-private joint venture, were submitted to the National Government for record after being discussed and decided by the Executive Yuan. Article 3 of the regulations states that after the market opens, no other business of the same or similar nature may be operated within the Shanghai municipal area. Article 2 of the market's operating regulations states that the types of fish traded in the fish market are stipulated as follows: (1) Marine fish, (2) Freshwater fish, (3) Dried fish, (4) Other aquatic products. The first transaction of the aforementioned fish entering Shanghai must be conducted in the fish market, etc. The appellant believed that the regulations and operating procedures were illegal and filed an appeal with the Ministry. Reason: Article 1 of the Appeal Law stipulates that people who have their rights or interests harmed by illegal or inappropriate actions by central or local government agencies may file an appeal. The appellant's intention in the appeal is that the fish market's regulations and operating procedures are illegal, requesting their revocation. This does not recognize that these regulations and operating procedures are a type of government plan for fisheries administration and do not impose any punishment on the appellant. Moreover, administrative orders are issued in order to benefit the majority of the people, and the people may not file an appeal against them. The circumstances of this case do not comply with the provisions of Article 1 of the Appeal Law. Therefore, the main text is decided according to law.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs the Ministry of Finance to Modify the Registration Deadline

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday to modify the deadline for registration and licensing. The original telegram stated: "Respectfully to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: It has been found that your ministry promulgated the Measures for Registration and Licensing of Wholesale, Purchasing, Transfer, and Inspection of Various Imported Goods' Businesses and Factories, and Transportation Companies. The licensing date stipulates in Article 2 that within 20 days from the date of promulgation of the measures in the local area, an application must be submitted to the agency designated by the Ministry of Finance for registration and licensing. Since the Chamber of Commerce received Announcement No. 1521 from the Jianghai Customs, forwarding the measures, it has immediately notified all industries to comply. However, the registration deadline is only 20 days. Many of the industries with smaller wholesale, purchasing, and transfer scales have failed to pay attention and have been unable to rush to complete the procedures on time. Failure to modify the procedures will inevitably make it impossible to continue business. Furthermore, the types of imported foreign goods that should be inspected have recently been modified and increased. The relevant industries affected by the increased portion still need to apply for registration and licensing in accordance with the measures. Therefore, the deadline in Article 2 of the law does in fact need to be extended. Therefore, we are specially telegraphing your ministry to review and approve, and order the Shanghai Customs to allow modification of the procedures for industries that apply for registration and licensing after the deadline, in order to alleviate commercial difficulties, which would be in the public interest. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

County Orders Reporting of Property Tax Reorganization

The property tax in various districts of Shanghai County was ordered to be reorganized. After receiving the order, the county government ordered the Public Security Bureau to comply. The bureau completed the investigation. The shop property tax, originally levied at 1.5%, has now been reduced to 1%. The households throughout the county are also uniformly collected in accordance with the regulations. All shops that previously concealed property values have been thoroughly investigated and earnestly reorganized. This year's implementation of collection will allocate the increased tax revenue for public security purposes. It is currently known that the bureau has received instructions from the county government to submit detailed reports on the progress of the property tax, such as the estimated number for this year, the number of households investigated for tax payment, the amount of tax to be collected each month, the amount of tax to be collected for the whole year, etc., so that the county can create a register and submit it to the provincial government for inspection and verification.

The Xu Wenliang Kidnapping Case; A Record of the Interrogation of the Bandits; Two Injured Bandits Have Recovered; Rescheduled for Further Trial on September 2

Xu Wenliang, the Cantonese manager of the Mei Foo Oil Company's kerosene department, was suddenly invaded by several armed bandits in his residence on YuYuan Road at around 3:00 AM on July 14. Xu was kidnapped and hidden in a bungalow at No. 1 Beihong Bridge Bank near Nanxiang, hoping to send a letter demanding a huge ransom. However, due to the lack of secrecy, Chief Detective Feng Baishun, Detectives Wang Yongjun, Sun Wenxi, and Wang Xichang, and Detectives Kong Guangxiao and Zhang Kuidong of the Chengdu Road Detective Bureau solved the case, arresting 11 male and female kidnappers and rescuing the hostage Xu Wenliang. It turned out that Wang Xichang's informant, Cao Chunbao, had participated in discussions about the kidnapping beforehand in order to report to the Detective Bureau afterward. Unfortunately, the bandit party learned of this, so when Xu Wenliang was kidnapped, Cao was taken along with him. After Xu Wenliang was kidnapped, Cao was severely injured in the eye by the bandit party using a gun butt. Cao had to go to the hospital for treatment, and the hospital reported it to the Detective Bureau. The detectives first arrested Cao and then, based on Cao's confession, successively arrested the kidnappers Lai Sheng, Zhang Heshang, Zhang Zefa, Zhang Xu, Yang Chunshan, Lu A'ge, Tang Heming, Shen Tingyan, Du Haisheng, and Chen Zhihong, totaling 11 people, and rescued the hostage. At the time, the criminal Shen Tingyan tried to escape across the bank and was shot and wounded by the detectives. Therefore, in addition to Shen and Cao Chunbao, who were left in the hospital, the remaining nine people were sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. It is now known that during the rescheduling of the case, the Chinese and Western detectives in charge of the case found that there were still three major criminals, Wang Jinsheng, Shen A'gen, Chen Weirong (i.e., "Lame Leg A'mao"), and "Long Legs Pudong Junior," at large. It was also found that the car with the Xiang Sheng number 18532 was hired by the bandit leader Wang Jinsheng to escort two accomplices to the bandit den to serve as guards. It was further determined that the defendant Yang Chunshan had, on July 13 of this year, led a gang to rob the home of Shu Mingdong at No. 41, Lane 807, Dixiwei Road, stealing 239 yuan in banknotes. It was also found that the defendant Chen Zhihong had provided a pistol and eight bullets to accomplices for robbery. Yesterday morning, the two injured defendants had recovered and were sent to the First Special Court together. The Detective Bureau's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, requested that the case be rescheduled for special interrogation because the circumstances of the case were tortuous and the number of people involved was large. Judge Tan ordered all the defendants to be remanded in custody and to be interrogated again on the afternoon of September 2.

A Rural Society report states that in the past seven or eight days, a disease has been discovered in the cattle in the Zhuanchiao, Beijiao, and Qianliangmiao areas of the suburbs of Shanghai. Sick cattle do not eat and make a moaning sound. They spread the disease to each other, which is very dangerous. In severe cases, they even die. Cattle are one of the farmers' assets, which is very important. Unfortunately, when cattle die, they wail endlessly. After hearing the news, Zhang Yi, Chairman of the Zhuanchiao Rural Improvement Association, immediately convened an emergency meeting and decided to send a letter to the Animal Husbandry Improvement Association for assistance. Dr. Cheng Shaohe, along with veterinarians, has gone to the countryside for diagnosis and will implement a method to prevent the spread of germs and inject serum into sick cattle to provide relief.

Yichang Jewelry Store Defrauded of Large Diamond Ring, Obtained a 500 Yuan Draft, No Such Bank Exists for Cashing

On the 20th of this month, around 2:00 PM, a customer dressed in luxurious clothing suddenly appeared at Yichang Jewelry Store, No. 19 Yuyuan Road in the city, wanting to purchase a large diamond ring. Zhao Rongshou (30 years old, from Suzhou), an employee of the store, immediately took out a solitaire diamond ring for the customer to choose from. Unexpectedly, the customer said that the money had to be collected in person at Yongxing Bank, No. 195 Xin Kaihe Road. Because Zhao was suffering from a foot ailment, the customer went upstairs and obtained a 500 yuan check from Geng Yu's bank and handed it to Zhao, but Zhao refused to accept it because he couldn't verify its authenticity. The customer said that Geng Yu was a large remittance bank, and he was the younger brother of the owner, named Zhang Qikun, and they could immediately go to Houma Road to cash the check. Zhao, seeing the large scale of the bank, took the check to cash it. However, after inquiring everywhere, no such bank existed, and he realized he had been deceived. He returned to Yongxing Bank, but Zhang had already fled. He inquired with the bank's cashier, Shen Fengyuan, who stated that there was no Zhang Qikun at the bank. Zhao then had to return to the store and report the situation to the Yemiao Police Station, requesting a strict investigation and arrest of the fraudulent bandits for prosecution.

Hotel Industry Held a General Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Extra Tips, Found It Difficult to Accept New Movement's Ban, Pushed Representatives to Express Hotel Industry's Plight

The Shanghai Hotel Industry Association held a temporary members' meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce meeting room at 3:00 PM yesterday to discuss the issue of extra tips. Representatives from the City Party Headquarters, Wang Longzhang, the City Chamber of Commerce, Yuan Hongjun, and over 200 representatives from hotels such as Central, Nanjing, Oriental, Jue Lu, and Shenzhou attended. The presidium, Chen Wenda, Sun Qiuping, Yan Rongqing, and Zheng Zhong, seriously discussed the matter, believing that, apart from voluntary tips from customers, extra solicitation by employees should not be allowed in principle. However, they found it very difficult to accept the implementation measures, which stipulated that security deposits and tips given by customers could not be collected and turned over as aviation donations. At the same time, employees also jointly appealed. The details of each situation are recorded below.

Chairman's Speech

Chairman Chen Wenda said in his opening remarks, "I am very honored that today's temporary meeting has been convened and that representatives from higher authorities and fellow industry members have attended enthusiastically. The purpose of convening this temporary meeting is to discuss an important issue concerning the survival of our industry, which is the elimination of extra tips in various industries, as advocated by the New Life Movement Promotion Association and widely publicized in society. A draft implementation plan has already been passed. We cannot criticize the elimination of extra tips in principle, but upon examining the facts, this issue is composed of various social factors and is extremely complex. We must comprehensively consider the practical difficulties and provide remedies, otherwise it will not only be of no practical benefit but may also cause major labor-management disputes. The weakness of China's industry and commerce, the difficulty of engaging in store operations, the hardships of employees' livelihoods, and the panic caused by store closures and bankruptcies, which increase employee unemployment, are all undeniable facts. Why are there extra tips? Because there is no fixed wage, or the wage is very meager, and employees have no choice but to rely on tips from customers to supplement their income. Why is there no fixed wage? Is it because the capitalists are exploiting them for their own benefit? No, absolutely not. Judging from the current situation in the industry, I can guarantee that over 90% are losing money. What is there to benefit from? On the contrary, the lives of employees are quite stable. This is evidenced by the facts. Therefore, the survival of the capitalists is even more urgent than that of the laborers. To eliminate extra tips, employees must, of course, have wages sufficient to maintain a minimum standard of living, and the capitalists must increase huge expenditures. And the huge expenditures will inevitably have to be compensated for by increasing selling prices. However, in the current situation where the social consumption capacity is declining, we only see painful auctions and large price reductions to attract customers. To increase selling prices is tantamount to going against society. Since increasing selling prices is impossible, what methods do the capitalists have to maintain this huge burden? If the capitalists cannot maintain it and go out of business, how will the employees live? Therefore, we must find a comprehensive method that takes into account both sides based on the principle of coexistence and mutual prosperity. In fact, the industry has always automatically eliminated extra tips. If a waiter serves diligently and gains the customer's favor and is rewarded, then the industry has no way to interfere. Because extra tips are not regulated, if a waiter has any extortionate behavior, they will offend the customer, and the store's business will also be affected, so it must be strictly corrected. As for the conditions of employment for waiters, such as treatment conditions and security deposits, these are a kind of contract between employer and employee, agreed upon by both parties. Any behavior agreed upon by both parties is a legal behavior. We deeply fear that while old habits should be reformed, we should also do our best to promote the New Life Movement, but we must start from the point of coexistence, mutual prosperity, and reducing disputes. As long as the store can barely maintain the minimum level of survival, they are happy to accept it and do not hope for profits. Please everyone contribute your valuable opinions and discuss a proper solution."

Resolution Process

After the chairman's report, representatives from higher authorities gave speeches. Then, according to the meeting agenda, discussions began. For the sake of seriousness, the chairman read aloud each item of the New Life Movement Promotion Association's plan to eliminate extra tips that had been passed. Then, the attending members studied each item one by one. Finally, considering everyone's opinions, the hotel industry cannot accept using the tips voluntarily given by customers as aviation donations because it concerns the business's existence and the employees' livelihoods. It was then resolved that the executive committee should submit the meeting's opinions and the hotel industry's plight to the City Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, and the Social Affairs Bureau for review and approval. Zhang Zhizhong, Sun Qiuping, Yan Rongzhong, Yao Songping, Chen Wenda, Ding Xin, Li Wencai, Sun Wenzhao, and Zhou Boyao were elected as representatives to the New Life Movement to express the hotel industry's plight.

Guard Wan Guosheng Abducted and Sold a Young Girl

Wan Guosheng, 30 years old, from Sichuan, previously served as a guard in a certain institution in Sichuan. In Sichuan, he had a relationship with Lu Huiying (21 years old), also from his hometown. However, Lu had already been betrothed to someone two years ago. For long-term plans, Wan secretly fled to Shanghai with the girl last month. The money he brought had already been completely used up. Wan could not think of any other way, and he brought the girl to a certain hotel in western Shanghai, preparing to sell her. Unexpectedly, the matter was discovered by Lu, who reported it to the local police station. The police ordered Wan's arrest and took him to the station for questioning. Wan's statements were evasive. The bureau believed that the case involved abduction and the sale of human beings, so they prepared a document and sent it to the general bureau for further investigation.

Burglary on Glock Road

No. 10 Xinmin Lane, Glock Road, French Concession, is the warehouse of Huamei Pharmacy, Fuzhou Road, Public Concession, where several employees and workers reside. At No. 72, Si'an Lane, Hengfeng Road, Robbers Opened Fire to Resist Arrest, Resulting in the Capture of Two Robbers and One Handgun

At 2:10 AM yesterday, four robbers speaking a Jiangbei dialect suddenly arrived at the home of Hong Daochang (56 years old, from Haizhou), a rickshaw puller who lived at No. 72, Si'an Lane, Hengfeng Road, Zhabei. One robber stood guard outside the door, while three robbers pried open the front door and entered the house. Two of the robbers each held a handgun, threatening and silencing the occupants. While they were rummaging through the boxes and chests upstairs, a worker downstairs who pulled rickshaws noticed and secretly ran out the back door to report to police officer Li Bingyu at post No. 2 of the Hengfeng Road Police Station, who reported it to the station. Police Chief Lu Pei immediately led patrol officers Huang and Hu, patrol leaders Gao Ziling, Zhang Fengtong, and Dai Jifu, detective Zhong Da, and others, a total of eleven people, each carrying box guns and handguns, to the scene. The robbers were about to flee when they were caught on the spot. Since the robber had no handgun, the patrol leaders were about to enter the homeowner's house when the robbers noticed and immediately opened fire to resist arrest. The sound of gunfire was as dense as a string of pearls, as if facing a major enemy. The long-term police officers in the police station all heard the sound and carried firearms to help. Patrol leader Gao Ziling was the most courageous, rushing up the stairs, grabbing one robber, and seizing one handgun. The remaining two robbers were chased to the third floor of an empty room at No. 117 before escaping. Afterwards, the two robbers captured were taken to the station. The handgun was inspected and found to be a six-inch Browning, serial number 92213, with three live rounds remaining and six rounds already fired. The robber on guard was immediately interrogated and identified himself as Wu Dasi, 23 years old, from Yancheng, living in a grass shed at No. 75, Tamziwankou, Zhabei, mainly pulling a rickshaw. The day before yesterday, in a barbershop opened by Zhang Mazi in Tamziwankou, Xiao Guozi, Xiao Manzi, and others agreed to rob No. 70 Si'an Lane this morning (yesterday morning). I stood guard at the door. Ming Rongsheng took a handgun with ten bullets in it. Unexpectedly, the plan went wrong and about ten shots were fired. Ming Rongsheng confessed that he was 27 years old, from Yancheng, pulling a rickshaw, and living in a grass shed at the Xiaocaichang in Tamziwan. The day before, Xiao Guozi said that the rickshaw company at No. 72 Si'an Lane had over a hundred yuan in business and was a good target. They gathered at the barbershop opened by Zhang Mazi and set off from the barbershop at a little past one o'clock this morning (yesterday morning). The handgun was mine. I went upstairs with Xiao Manzi. I only robbed 6.2 yuan in banknotes and 400 copper coins. I don't know about the banknotes and clothes. On June 20th of this year, at 9:00 PM, I robbed Guisenji Cigarette Paper Shop at No. 1601 Jiaotong Road. On May 1st, at 8:30 PM, I robbed Taichang Southern Goods Store in Panjiwan. The police officer there was from post 45, officer number 1748. On May 11th, at about 9:00 PM, I robbed the grass shed at No. 126 behind the Nanyang Soap Factory on Zhongxing Road. After the confession was obtained, the owners of Guisenji Cigarette Paper Shop on Jiaotong Road, the owner of Taichang Southern Goods Store, and the owner of the grass shed on Zhongxing Road were immediately summoned to inquire and confirmed the information. The homeowner of the rickshaw company in Si'an Lane, Hong Daochang, reported that he was robbed of over 40 yuan in silver and banknotes and several pieces of clothing. Further investigation and arrest of the remaining accomplices are currently underway.

Sister's Death Causes Grief, Brother Commits Suicide by Poison

Zhong Ahua, 26 years old, from Ningbo, a plasterer by trade, came to Shanghai to make a living. He resided with his older sister at No. 1 Beidi Lane, Beidi Road, French Concession. His sister passed away due to illness a month ago. On the 22nd of this month, the traditional sixth seven-day period after death, after Zhong prepared a meal for his sister, he was overcome with the thought that he had no one to rely on after his sister's death. Grief welled up within him, and after weeping for a while, he had a fleeting thought and committed suicide by swallowing raw opium. At 4:00 PM that afternoon, the poison took effect, and his sister's husband, Gu Yongxian, discovered him and called his brother, Zhong Junyu, to help send him to Renji Hospital. Because he had been poisoned deeply, the treatment was ineffective, and he died at 10:20 AM yesterday. The hospital reported it to the French police station, who sent detectives to investigate. They transferred the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch autopsy room to await inspection by the Second Special Court today.

Kicking a Pregnant Woman at the Door, Zhang Mingqian Detained Pending Trial

Zhang Mingqian, 52 years old, from Haimen, residing at No. 48, Jianye Lane, Fuli Road, French Concession, his son, Yu Sheng, 12 years old, had an argument and scuffle with his neighbor's son, De Sui, in the courtyard a few days ago. Zhang intervened, causing him to kick and injure Yang Chen, the pregnant wife of Yang Dasan, 29 years old, from Tongzhou, who lived at No. 49, Kunlin Lane, in the same neighborhood. The victim's family reported it to the French police station, who sent Chen to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Detective Le Sixiang arrested Zhang, and previously sent him to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The Legal Affairs Office lawyer, Chen Men, presented the case, stating that the victim was being treated in the hospital and requesting a postponement of the investigation before filing for trial. Judge Zhang interrogated Zhang Mingqian, then ordered that the interrogation be postponed until the victim recovered from her injuries, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

Rope Breaks, Workman Falls to Death

The Catholic Shoushan Hall at No. 44 Sapo Sai Road, French Concession, recently hired a workman from Meihe Foreign Firm at No. 261 Jiangxi Road to repair the roof. Around 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, a workman, Xia Agou, 33 years old, from Shaoxing, was standing on the roof's eaves of the four-story building, helping the workers below to lift stones to the roof, when the thick rope suddenly broke. Xia was hit by the broken rope and lost his balance, falling to the ground from a height. He injured his head, broke his right leg, and immediately fainted, losing consciousness. He was sent to Guangci Hospital, but it was too late for treatment, and he died at 2:00 AM that night. The French police station received a report and sent detectives to investigate, transferring the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch autopsy room. The next day, Prosecutor Wang Ren of the Second Special Court arrived at the scene to confirm that the death was due to injuries sustained in the fall. The body was claimed by his brother, Xia Axiang, for burial.

Fish Market's New Retail Market to Be Completed Next Month

The Shanghai Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry, in order to expand its business, is constructing a retail market. It has already contracted with merchants this month for a price of over 30,000 yuan. The entire building is located next to the Fish Market office and occupies a large area. The roof is made of sheet iron, with cement poured underneath. There are a total of eight sections, with ten rooms in each section, for a total of eighty rooms. It is expected to be completed next month. In the future, all retail matters related to the market can be transacted in the retail market.

Dr. Li Zhejun Returns to China

Dr. Li Zhejun, a female physician, graduated from Tongde Medical College in Shanghai in her early years. She has served in the Jiangsu Provincial Hospital, the World Red Swastika Society Hospital, and the Suzhou Chunquan Clinic, presiding over medical affairs and enjoying a high reputation. However, the doctor was not satisfied with this and was determined to further her studies. In the spring of the 24th year, she went to Japan and entered Tokyo Izumibashi Hospital, studying under the famous physician Dr. Murakami, specializing in gynecology and obstetrics, and interning in surgery at the hospital, gaining much experience. She returned to China on the 20th from Yokohama on the British Empress of Asia ship, arriving in Shanghai this morning. She will surely make a contribution to the medical community in her homeland.

Tang Zhenxu Departs Overseas Today

Mr. Tang Zhenxu, a native of Wuxi, Jiangsu, is 26 years old and the eldest son of Tang Mufen, a member of the National Government Zhen Committee. In June of last year, he graduated from the Department of Civil Engineering and Hydraulic Engineering of the Tangshan College of Engineering of the National Jiaotong University, earning a bachelor's degree. He was assigned by the Ministry of Railways to serve in the Engineering Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways. He was then temporarily transferred to Shandong Dongcheng Township, where he served as an engineer on the Yellow River Dongzhuang Flood Control Engineering Committee, gaining rich experience in Yellow River hydrology and

Mr. Tang Zhenxu

China's embankment advancement and the old and new methods of dike closure. After the closure of the Dongzhuang opening, he was introduced by Zhu Ziqiao and Li Yizhi to travel extensively through Shaanxi, studying the actual facilities of irrigation projects in the Jinghui, Weihui, and Luohui Canals, seeing the actual facilities of irrigation projects in our country. He will depart overseas to the United States on the 24th of this month on the British Changxing Company's Japanese Empress ship, entering the Graduate School of Cornell University to specialize in hydraulic engineering, so as to enrich his knowledge.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the area around Shandong is overcast with showers and strong northeasterly winds. The Yellow River basin and the upper reaches of the Yangtze River are experiencing good weather with light and variable winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have northwesterly to northeasterly winds. The East Sea and Taiwan are cloudy with unstable winds. The Pacific hurricane remains stationary, its center at 2:00 PM yesterday was located within approximately 120 miles of 20 degrees North latitude and 16 degrees East longitude. Another hurricane northwest of Guam had its center at 2:00 PM yesterday located within approximately 120 miles of 18 degrees North latitude and 137 degrees East longitude, moving northwest-west. The strength of both hurricanes is not fully known. Furthermore, the highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 89.6 degrees, and the lowest was 75.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 95.9 degrees, and the lowest was 77.0 degrees.

Konti Huacheng Cup Doubles Tournament: Carson and Squiers Win the Championship; Beat He Jialiu and Liu Jie 3-2 Yesterday; He Jialiu Failed Despite Winning Back Two Sets

The final of the Konti Open Tennis Huacheng Cup Doubles between He Jialiu and Liu Jie versus Carson and Squiers took place at the Konti Club court at 4 PM yesterday. The competition was fierce. In the end, the He-Liu team narrowly lost 2-3. The Carson-Squiers team was fortunate to win the championship. It is noted that Carson also won the Huacheng Cup Singles Championship. The battle is described below:

Carson and Squiers Win Two Consecutive Sets

After the start of the match, Carson served, and He took the lead bravely. However, due to a momentary lapse, the Carson-Squiers team surpassed them with a score of 2-1. But He and Liu immediately tied the score. Afterwards, there were two more ties at 3-3 and 4-4, but the Carson-Squiers team always took the lead. In the ninth and tenth games, after fierce fighting, victory belonged to Carson and Squiers. He and Liu lost the first set with a score of 4-6. In the second set, Squiers served and won the first game. Then Liu, Carson, and He also won by serving. At this time, the opportunities were equal. The He-Liu team was very confident with their shots. After a score of 2-3, the situation deteriorated rapidly, and the Carson-Squiers team won four consecutive games. He and Liu then lost the second set with a score of 2-6.

He and Liu Regain Momentum

After Carson and Squiers won two consecutive sets, the third set became a matter of life and death for the He-Liu team. In the first game, the He-Liu team proceeded smoothly and took the lead. Unexpectedly, Carson and Squiers surpassed them again with a score of 2-1. After 2-1, Carson and Squiers led 4-2, and the situation became extremely dangerous. He and Liu responded calmly, and they gradually improved. After winning three consecutive games, they took control of the overall situation with a score of 5-4. Unexpectedly, Carson and Squiers tied the score again at 5-5, and the situation transitioned through stormy seas again. Finally, He and Liu were successful in their efforts and won back the second set with a score of 7-5, offering a glimmer of hope. In the fourth set, He and Liu were even more fierce, winning the first two games. Carson and Squiers tried hard to catch up but were unable to surpass them. The overall situation was controlled by He and Liu. At 5-4, the tension was even greater. He and Liu intercepted at the net, and the drop points demonstrated ingenuity. They won the fourth set with a score of 6-4, saving the critical situation.

Final Credit for the Victory

After winning two sets, the situation became evenly matched. The last set was the deciding set and the focus of the competition for both sides. However, after forty games of fierce fighting, He and Liu were visibly exhausted. Although they still fought hard, Carson and Squiers took advantage of every key moment. After losing three consecutive games, they only managed to win back one set. But Carson and Squiers quickly made a sharp turn, suddenly leading 5-1. He and Liu's hopes were once again slim. But He and Liu were ultimately a strong team. At the critical moment of success or failure, they remained extremely calm. Indeed, they won two consecutive games, bringing the score back to 5-3. Unexpectedly, Carson served again in the ninth game, and the serves were as fast as bullets. Although He and Liu returned the ball over the net twice, their efforts ultimately failed to achieve success. In the end, Ai (He?) lost miserably with a score of 3-6, and Carson and Squiers narrowly won the Huacheng Cup Doubles Championship with a score of 3-2.

World Games Award Ceremony

Fragments of World Games Track and Field Judging and Equipment

—Jiang Lianggui from Berlin

The 11th World Games opened solemnly and enthusiastically at the National Sports Center in the suburbs of Berlin. The reporter traveled from his hometown 24,000 miles away, circling half the globe, passing through Africa and arriving in Europe to participate in the grand event. This is such a joyful thing.

The scale of the entire Olympic Games is magnificent, and the thoroughness of the handling is truly beyond our expectations. No matter which aspect, under any tense situation, we have never encountered any clumsy or chaotic situations. There are very few staff members, but they all make the most of their work efficiency and achieve the goal of making the best use of their talents. In terms of handling affairs, everything feels worthy of reporting, so that it can be used as a reference for sports colleagues in the hometown. But this is absolutely impossible. Now, first, based on what I saw on the first day in the track and field arena, from the perspective of the sports world, I will discuss a few small issues with my colleagues in the country.

High Jump

Passing under the bar after jumping over it does not constitute a foul. This is something that people don't pay attention to, but the reporter felt very happy after discovering it. In the past, when working in the country, many disputes arose over this matter. Many sports colleagues, when officiating track and field competitions, always had a rule saying, "Athletes in high jump and pole vault who pass over the bar and then run back under the bar will be considered a failure." In fact, this clause is not listed in the rules, but everyone almost followed it by misinterpretation. Therefore, I paid special attention to this point at this World Games. Fortunately, the first event was high jump. As a result, I found that most athletes ran back under the bar after jumping over it. The referees treated it as if there was no rule. Of course, we can trust that this was not a referee's oversight, but because there is no such clause in the rules. What I have often doubted for several years has received a satisfactory answer. At the same time, there are not a few people in the country who feel the same as the reporter. From then on, there can be a uniform method for this exceptional rule.

Measurement of High Jump

(1) The Height Increased Each Time This is also something that is not unified. At domestic sports meets, I have never heard of any regulations on the increase in high jump height. Everyone does what they want without any fixed rules. Of course, the uneven increase in height each time is definitely not beneficial to the athletes. At this World Games, the official competition's starting height was 1 meter 85, and each increase was 0.03 meters (three centimeters). I think this is a very appropriate height. In smaller sports meets, the starting height may be slightly reduced, but the increased height can be consistent. (2) Height Measurement Height measurement is a very troublesome and difficult task to achieve accurately. The method used at this conference is relatively accurate and simple, and it is also very economical and can be imitated. (This method is also used in China, but it is not very common.) The method uses a triangular wooden block, about two meters thirty long, with a wooden base. The wood is extremely strong, and the height is engraved on it, with centimeters as the unit. Each time the height is measured, you only need to place the height wood on the bar and view the height from a parallel line.

Javelin

(1) Communication of Errors The javelin throw is thrown from a long distance. At the same time, the line referee and the distance referee must communicate with each other. After each athlete throws, the line referee must inform the distance referee. If there is no appropriate signal and a megaphone is used to communicate, the referees are easily fatigued, and the audience is easily annoyed by the noisy sounds in the field. During the competition, red and white flags can be used. After the athlete throws, if he does not cross the line, raise the white flag to indicate credibility, and the measurer can measure. If he crosses the line, raise the red flag. This method not only makes it difficult for the referees to misunderstand, but also allows the entire audience to see it clearly.

(2) The Thrower Retrieves the Javelin Himself After the javelin is thrown, the athlete's forward trend is determined, so he runs to retrieve it himself. (The benefit of this approach is to reduce the number of people on the field, avoid danger, and allow them to know their distance. Although the method is desirable, it should not be used in situations where the scale is small, the sports meet is short, the number of people is large, and time is limited.

Referees

(1) The athletes of each event are led out of the field by the referees of each event. This is one of the things that makes me most satisfied. Every time we hold a sports meet in the country, we feel that the most difficult thing is to maintain order on the field. Every time we hold a sports meet, there are not many nominally appointed officials who leisurely walk around the field, looking around, or many retired athletes (the projects have been completed, forming groups and walking back and forth endlessly. The progress of the sports meet is affected, and the audience's line of sight is also obstructed. The method used at this conference is excellent. The athletes of each event report at the roll call point at the specified time, and the referees in charge of each event lead them into the field in a line. When the entire event is over, the referees of that event lead them out of the field in a line. Therefore, there are no idle officials watching the competition in the field, and no retired athletes running around. The order is orderly.

(2) Issuing Membership Clothing The issuer has the greatest impact on performance. At this World Games, the clothing issued to the issuers is different from that of general referees. They wear white coats, like doctors, which are very obvious. Athletes, spectators, and referees can all see it clearly at a glance.

(3) Finish Line Referee Platform The platform is different from what is seen in China. Most of what is seen in China are two meters wide, and each level can seat three people. Here, it is different. The platform is extremely narrow, and each level can only seat two people. This method is more advanced, because if three people sit on one level at the same time, only one person can get the most accurate line of sight, and the other two will have some differences. Only "people" sit on each level, so each person is in the most excellent position.

Distance Markers

Use hexagonal wooden blocks instead of small flags, because lead flags can only be seen by the audience on both sides, while hexagonal wooden blocks can be seen by the audience on all four sides.

Performance Report

(1) When the competition is in progress, for track and field events in progress, each throw is reported immediately. The method is to set up two reporting boards on the ground at each of the four corners of the field, one for the athlete's number plate and one for the performance plate. Each corner has two people handling the matter. Each corner has a telephone. Every time the athlete throws, the number is reported first, and the score is also marked immediately. The process is extremely fast, and the entire audience can know the exact distance of each athlete's throw.

(2) The results of track races are reported on the general reporting board after each race is completed. The scores of each person are marked.

Photography

For track races, the finish line photo is washed out within five minutes of each race. The speed of handling is extremely fast, so the photographic equipment must be as complete as possible. However, it must not obstruct the audience. The method is quite good. Obstacles are attached to the finish line, and pits are dug on the left and right sides of the track and field field, about a foot from the ground. The camera is placed in the pit. The position is good and does not obstruct the audience's line of sight.

Educational News

Various Provinces and Cities: Implementation of Educational Film Methods - Free Admission as the Principle for Educational Film Screenings

The Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities on the 22nd, stating that films are a powerful tool for promoting social education and assisting school education. Recognizing this, the Ministry has established a Film Education Committee to oversee the matter, including training projectionists, purchasing equipment, and producing films. Instructions have been issued or are being actively planned. In order to urge universal implementation, special measures for the implementation of educational films in various provinces and cities have been formulated to facilitate progress. In addition to separate orders, the relevant measures are enclosed for compliance. Plans for the delimitation of educational film tour screening districts in the counties under their jurisdiction, and the fundraising for all expenses, should also be prepared in advance and submitted for review. This order is hereby issued.

Measures for the Implementation of Educational Films in Various Provinces and Cities: 1. The Ministry of Education has formulated these measures to urge the implementation of film education in various provinces and cities. 2. To promote the universal implementation of film education, the education departments and bureaus (or social bureaus) of each province and city shall designate one staff member in the relevant social education department to handle film education administration (which may also handle radio education matters). Each province shall also delineate educational film tour screening districts within its territory, establish projection teams in each district, and handle the screening of educational films. 3. Educational film tour projectionists and assistants shall be appointed by the education departments and bureaus of each province and city, but the appointment of projectionists shall be limited to personnel trained and certified by the Ministry of Education. The service regulations will be determined separately. 4. Each educational film tour screening district shall have one projectionist and one assistant, and shall be equipped with the following equipment: (1) 16mm projector; (2) household generator (110V AC 50W); (3) projector bulbs (spare); (4) screen; (5) miscellaneous items (splicing tape, cleaning fluid, oil, pliers, chisels, etc.). The cost of the above items is approximately 1,000 yuan, which is the necessary equipment for film screenings and shall be set up in each district. (6) Slide projector; (7) public address system (110V AC); (8) records. The above items are auxiliary equipment and may be postponed if funding is limited. 5. Projectors and equipment, excluding items (4) and (5), shall be purchased or manufactured by the Ministry of Education and distributed to the education departments and bureaus of each province and city for procurement at cost. (6) The salaries of projectionists and assistants, the cost of purchasing equipment, and operating expenses shall be covered by the education funds of each province and city. However, provinces with genuine funding difficulties may be subsidized by the Ministry of Education for a portion of the equipment purchase costs at its discretion. 7. Educational films shall be distributed free of charge by the Ministry of Education. The distribution method will be determined separately. 8. Educational film tour projectionists shall distribute the screening dates evenly among the counties and cities in the district. Upon arrival in a county or city, they shall consult with the county and city

New Disciplinary Plan at Zhengfeng Middle School

Zhengfeng Middle School in Xujiahui in this city has been established for ten years. Since Wu Kaixian took over as chairman of the board and Hu Changzhi took over as principal last year, the school's operations have developed further. There are currently more than 400 students and more than 40 faculty and staff members. The facilities are well-equipped, and the academic atmosphere is excellent. Recently, Principal Hu of the school announced a new disciplinary plan for the coming year to various newspapers. The following is a selection of the original text:

When the school was first founded, it was a time when normal academic habits were rampant and morale was low. The school's purpose in establishing itself was to express its unique spirit and realize its unique ideals in the midst of this universally turbulent and evil trend. The reason why the two characters "Zhengfeng" (正風, meaning "correcting the wind") were adopted as the school's name is for this reason. However, since the school was founded ten years ago, the ills of society have remained, and the effectiveness of running the school has not been evident. Although the comrades who run the school and the students of the school can frequently sound the morning rooster in a common environment of study and mutual encouragement, but as the saying goes, "the Way is one foot high, but the demons are ten feet high." The efforts of individuals ultimately cannot withstand the changes in society. The fact that the spirit of our school has failed to attract social attention is also a major reason. For a year now, the school has faced this problem, studied it in depth, and invited teachers from all levels of the school, as well as educational experts from various places, to provide opinions and jointly review them. Combining public opinion, it is generally believed that the power of society is indeed great, but the school's failure to cultivate students to perfection is still one of the reasons. From the school's point of view, it is still necessary to put in a lot of effort in this regard. The school is built on its words, and it has been decided that from the next semester onwards, a Student Life Guidance Committee will be established in the school's administrative system, alongside the Dean of Students' Office, to jointly assume full responsibility for the school's disciplinary education. In general, the mission of the Dean of Students' Office belongs to the negative aspect, and the mission of the Student Life Guidance Committee belongs to the positive aspect. In other words, the two institutions of the Dean of Students' Office and the Student Life Guidance Committee will implement a kind of rigid control method over all aspects of student life. The scientific basis for this kind of life control lies in basing it on the research results of physiology and psychology, and making a reasonable allocation of students' daily life, such as the length of reading time, the amount of sleep and rest, and the proportion of games and homework. With this method, students can abide by discipline and regulations in their school life, and perhaps in the future, after leaving school, they can use their learning to correct society. The spirit of the school can be carried forward and developed. At the beginning of this implementation, we sincerely hope that people from all walks of life will give us serious criticism and reasonable guidance.
